FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS
Match Result (1X2)
Both Teams to Score
Totals (Over/Under)
Correct Score
Half-Time / Full-Time
Handicaps
LIVE (IN-PLAY) BETTING

Live betting markets typically include:

Next Team to Score
Next Goalscorer
Live Match Result
Live Totals (Over/Under)

Live odds update continuously based on match events, momentum and tactical decisions.

LAST 10 WORLD CUP WINNERS
Year	Host Country	Winner	Runner-Up
2022	Qatar	Argentina	France
2018	Russia	France	Croatia
2014	Brazil	Germany	Argentina
2010	South Africa	Spain	Netherlands
2006	Germany	Italy	France
2002	South Korea/Japan	Brazil	Germany
1998	France	France	Brazil
1994	United States	Brazil	Italy
1990	Italy	West Germany	Argentina
1986	Mexico	Argentina	West Germany
WORLD CUP TOP GOALSCORER

Who will collect the Golden Boot at the 2026 World Cup? Will it be a superstar youngster like Bukayo Saka or Argentina’s Julian Alvarez? What impact will megastars Erling Haaland and Kylian Mbappé have? Or will someone from the veteran side of things like England’s Harry Kane, Brazil’s Neymar or the great Lionel Messi do the business?

TOP GOALSCORERS FROM THE LAST FIVE WORLD CUP EDITIONS

WORLD CUP 2026 FAQ
WHEN DOES THE 2026 WORLD CUP START?

The tournament starts on Thursday, 11 June 2026.

WHEN IS THE WORLD CUP FINAL?

The final will be played on Sunday, 19 July 2026.

WHERE IS THE 2026 WORLD CUP HOSTED?

Canada, Mexico and the United States.

HOW MANY TEAMS AND MATCHES ARE INVOLVED?

48 teams and 104 matches.

FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination

To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS

Both Teams to Score

World Cup 2026
FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS
Match Result (1X2)
Both Teams to Score
Totals (Over/Under)
Correct Score
Half-Time / Full-Time
Handicaps
LIVE (IN-PLAY) BETTING

Live betting markets typically include:

Next Team to Score
Next Goalscorer
Live Match Result
Live Totals (Over/Under)

Live odds update continuously based on match events, momentum and tactical decisions.

World Cup 2026
FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS

Live odds update continuously based on match events, momentum and tactical decisions.

Who will collect the Golden Boot at the 2026 World Cup? Will it be a superstar youngster like Bukayo Saka or Argentina’s Julian Alvarez? What impact will megastars Erling Haaland and Kylian Mbappé have? Or will someone from the veteran side of things like England’s Harry Kane, Brazil’s Neymar or the great Lionel Messi do the business?

World Cup 2026
FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS

Or will someone from the veteran side of things like England’s Harry Kane, Brazil’s Neymar or the great Lionel Messi do the business?

World Cup 2026
FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS
Match Result (1X2)
Both Teams to Score
Totals (Over/Under)
Correct Score
Half-Time / Full-Time
Handicaps
LIVE (IN-PLAY) BETTING

Live betting markets typically include:

Next Team to Score
Next Goalscorer
Live Match Result
Live Totals (Over/Under)

Live odds update continuously based on match events, momentum and tactical decisions.

2018	Russia	France	Croatia
2014	Brazil	Germany	Argentina
2010	South Africa	Spain	Netherlands

2002	South Korea/Japan	Brazil	Germany
1998	France	France	Brazil
1994	United States	Brazil	Italy
1990	Italy	West Germany	Argentina
1986	Mexico	Argentina	West Germany
WORLD CUP TOP GOALSCORER

Who will collect the Golden Boot at the 2026 World Cup? Will it be a superstar youngster like Bukayo Saka or Argentina’s Julian Alvarez? What impact will megastars Erling Haaland and Kylian Mbappé have? Or will someone from the veteran side of things like England’s Harry Kane, Brazil’s Neymar or the great Lionel Messi do the business?

The final will be played on Sunday, 19 July 2026.

Canada, Mexico and the United States.

World Cup 2026
FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS
Match Result (1X2)
Both Teams to Score
Totals (Over/Under)
Correct Score
Half-Time / Full-Time
Handicaps
LIVE (IN-PLAY) BETTING

Live betting markets typically include:

Next Team to Score
Next Goalscorer
Live Match Result
Live Totals (Over/Under)

Live odds update continuously based on match events, momentum and tactical decisions.

World Cup 2026
FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination

To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

World Cup 2026
FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS
Match Result (1X2)
Both Teams to Score
Totals (Over/Under)
Correct Score
Half-Time / Full-Time
Handicaps
LIVE (IN-PLAY) BETTING

Live betting markets typically include:

Next Team to Score
Next Goalscorer
Live Match Result
Live Totals (Over/Under)

Live odds update continuously based on match events, momentum and tactical decisions.

LAST 10 WORLD CUP WINNERS
Year	Host Country	Winner	Runner-Up
2022	Qatar	Argentina	France
2018	Russia	France	Croatia
2014	Brazil	Germany	Argentina
2010	South Africa	Spain	Netherlands
2006	Germany	Italy	France
2002	South Korea/Japan	Brazil	Germany
1998	France	France	Brazil
1994	United States	Brazil	Italy
1990	Italy	West Germany	Argentina
1986	Mexico	Argentina	West Germany
WORLD CUP TOP GOALSCORER

Who will collect the Golden Boot at the 2026 World Cup? Will it be a superstar youngster like Bukayo Saka or Argentina’s Julian Alvarez? What impact will megastars Erling Haaland and Kylian Mbappé have? Or will someone from the veteran side of things like England’s Harry Kane, Brazil’s Neymar or the great Lionel Messi do the business?

TOP GOALSCORERS FROM THE LAST FIVE WORLD CUP EDITIONS

WORLD CUP 2026 FAQ
WHEN DOES THE 2026 WORLD CUP START?

The tournament starts on Thursday, 11 June 2026.

WHEN IS THE WORLD CUP FINAL?

The final will be played on Sunday, 19 July 2026.

WHERE IS THE 2026 WORLD CUP HOSTED?

Canada, Mexico and the United States.

HOW MANY TEAMS AND MATCHES ARE INVOLVED?

48 teams and 104 matches.

World Cup 2026
FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS
Match Result (1X2)
Both Teams to Score
Totals (Over/Under)

What impact will megastars Erling Haaland and Kylian Mbappé have? Or will someone from the veteran side of things like England’s Harry Kane, Brazil’s Neymar or the great Lionel Messi do the business?

World Cup 2026
FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS
Match Result (1X2)
Both Teams to Score
Totals (Over/Under)
Correct Score
Half-Time / Full-Time
Handicaps
LIVE (IN-PLAY) BETTING

Live betting markets typically include:

Next Team to Score
Next Goalscorer
Live Match Result
Live Totals (Over/Under)

Live odds update continuously based on match events, momentum and tactical decisions.

What impact will megastars Erling Haaland and Kylian Mbappé have? Or will someone from the veteran side of things like England’s Harry Kane, Brazil’s Neymar or the great Lionel Messi do the business?

World Cup 2026
FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS
Match Result (1X2)
Both Teams to Score
Totals (Over/Under)
Correct Score
Half-Time / Full-Time
Handicaps
LIVE (IN-PLAY) BETTING

Live betting markets typically include:

Next Team to Score
Next Goalscorer
Live Match Result
Live Totals (Over/Under)

Live odds update continuously based on match events, momentum and tactical decisions.

World Cup 2026
FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final

What impact will megastars Erling Haaland and Kylian Mbappé have? Or will someone from the veteran side of things like England’s Harry Kane, Brazil’s Neymar or the great Lionel Messi do the business?

World Cup 2026
FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS

Or will someone from the veteran side of things like England’s Harry Kane, Brazil’s Neymar or the great Lionel Messi do the business?

World Cup 2026
FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS
Match Result (1X2)
Both Teams to Score
Totals (Over/Under)
Correct Score
Half-Time / Full-Time
Handicaps
LIVE (IN-PLAY) BETTING

Live betting markets typically include:

Next Team to Score
Next Goalscorer
Live Match Result
Live Totals (Over/Under)

Live odds update continuously based on match events, momentum and tactical decisions.

2018	Russia	France	Croatia
2014	Brazil	Germany	Argentina
2010	South Africa	Spain	Netherlands
2006	Germany	Italy	France
2002	South Korea/Japan	Brazil	Germany
1998	France	France	Brazil
1994	United States	Brazil	Italy
1990	Italy	West Germany	Argentina
1986	Mexico	Argentina	West Germany
WORLD CUP TOP GOALSCORER

Who will collect the Golden Boot at the 2026 World Cup? Will it be a superstar youngster like Bukayo Saka or Argentina’s Julian Alvarez? What impact will megastars Erling Haaland and Kylian Mbappé have? Or will someone from the veteran side of things like England’s Harry Kane, Brazil’s Neymar or the great Lionel Messi do the business?

The final will be played on Sunday, 19 July 2026.

WHERE IS THE 2026 WORLD CUP HOSTED?

Canada, Mexico and the United States.

World Cup 2026
FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS
Match Result (1X2)
Both Teams to Score
Totals (Over/Under)
Correct Score
Half-Time / Full-Time
Handicaps
LIVE (IN-PLAY) BETTING

Live betting markets typically include:

Next Team to Score
Next Goalscorer
Live Match Result
Live Totals (Over/Under)

Live odds update continuously based on match events, momentum and tactical decisions.

World Cup 2026
FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination

To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

World Cup 2026
FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS
Match Result (1X2)
Both Teams to Score
Totals (Over/Under)
Correct Score
Half-Time / Full-Time
Handicaps
LIVE (IN-PLAY) BETTING

Live betting markets typically include:

Next Team to Score
Next Goalscorer

Live Totals (Over/Under)

Live odds update continuously based on match events, momentum and tactical decisions.

LAST 10 WORLD CUP WINNERS
Year	Host Country	Winner	Runner-Up
2022	Qatar	Argentina	France
2018	Russia	France	Croatia
2014	Brazil	Germany	Argentina
2010	South Africa	Spain	Netherlands
2006	Germany	Italy	France
2002	South Korea/Japan	Brazil	Germany
1998	France	France	Brazil
1994	United States	Brazil	Italy
1990	Italy	West Germany	Argentina
1986	Mexico	Argentina	West Germany
WORLD CUP TOP GOALSCORER

Who will collect the Golden Boot at the 2026 World Cup? Will it be a superstar youngster like Bukayo Saka or Argentina’s Julian Alvarez? What impact will megastars Erling Haaland and Kylian Mbappé have? Or will someone from the veteran side of things like England’s Harry Kane, Brazil’s Neymar or the great Lionel Messi do the business?

TOP GOALSCORERS FROM THE LAST FIVE WORLD CUP EDITIONS

WORLD CUP 2026 FAQ
WHEN DOES THE 2026 WORLD CUP START?

The tournament starts on Thursday, 11 June 2026.

WHEN IS THE WORLD CUP FINAL?

The final will be played on Sunday, 19 July 2026.

WHERE IS THE 2026 WORLD CUP HOSTED?

Canada, Mexico and the United States.

HOW MANY TEAMS AND MATCHES ARE INVOLVED?

48 teams and 104 matches.

FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS
Match Result (1X2)
Both Teams to Score
Totals (Over/Under)
Correct Score
Half-Time / Full-Time
Handicaps
LIVE (IN-PLAY) BETTING

Live betting markets typically include:

Next Team to Score
Next Goalscorer
Live Match Result
Live Totals (Over/Under)

Live odds update continuously based on match events, momentum and tactical decisions.

1998	France	France	Brazil
1994	United States	Brazil	Italy
1990	Italy	West Germany	Argentina
1986	Mexico	Argentina	West Germany
WORLD CUP TOP GOALSCORER

Who will collect the Golden Boot at the 2026 World Cup? Will it be a superstar youngster like Bukayo Saka or Argentina’s Julian Alvarez? What impact will megastars Erling Haaland and Kylian Mbappé have? Or will someone from the veteran side of things like England’s Harry Kane, Brazil’s Neymar or the great Lionel Messi do the business?

The tournament starts on Thursday, 11 June 2026.

WHEN IS THE WORLD CUP FINAL?

The final will be played on Sunday, 19 July 2026.

WHERE IS THE 2026 WORLD CUP HOSTED?

Canada, Mexico and the United States.

48 teams and 104 matches.

FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS
Match Result (1X2)
Both Teams to Score
Totals (Over/Under)
Correct Score
Half-Time / Full-Time
Handicaps
LIVE (IN-PLAY) BETTING

Live betting markets typically include:

Next Team to Score
Next Goalscorer
Live Match Result
Live Totals (Over/Under)

Live odds update continuously based on match events, momentum and tactical decisions.

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS

Or will someone from the veteran side of things like England’s Harry Kane, Brazil’s Neymar or the great Lionel Messi do the business?

FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS
Match Result (1X2)
Both Teams to Score
Totals (Over/Under)
Correct Score
Half-Time / Full-Time
Handicaps
LIVE (IN-PLAY) BETTING

Live betting markets typically include:

Next Team to Score
Next Goalscorer
Live Match Result
Live Totals (Over/Under)

Live odds update continuously based on match events, momentum and tactical decisions.

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination

To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS

FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS
Match Result (1X2)
Both Teams to Score
Totals (Over/Under)
Correct Score
Half-Time / Full-Time
Handicaps
LIVE (IN-PLAY) BETTING

Live betting markets typically include:

Next Team to Score
Next Goalscorer

Live Totals (Over/Under)

Live odds update continuously based on match events, momentum and tactical decisions.

FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS
Match Result (1X2)
Both Teams to Score
Totals (Over/Under)
Correct Score
Half-Time / Full-Time
Handicaps
LIVE (IN-PLAY) BETTING

Live betting markets typically include:

Next Team to Score
Next Goalscorer
Live Match Result
Live Totals (Over/Under)

Live odds update continuously based on match events, momentum and tactical decisions.

The tournament starts on Thursday, 11 June 2026.

WHEN IS THE WORLD CUP FINAL?

The final will be played on Sunday, 19 July 2026.

WHERE IS THE 2026 WORLD CUP HOSTED?

Canada, Mexico and the United States.

HOW MANY TEAMS AND MATCHES ARE INVOLVED?

48 teams and 104 matches.

FIFA WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING ODDS

The FIFA World Cup 2026 will be the largest edition of the tournament ever staged. For the first time, the competition will feature 48 teams, expanding the tournament to a total of 104 matches and increasing betting opportunities across all stages.

The tournament will take place between June and July 2026. According to FIFA, the opening match will be played on Thursday, 11 June 2026, while the World Cup Final is scheduled for Sunday, 19 July 2026.

OFFICIAL WORLD CUP 2026 FACTS
Tournament dates: Thursday, 11 June 2026 – Sunday, 19 July 2026
Total teams: 48
Total matches: 104
Host countries: Canada, Mexico and the United States
HOSTS: CANADA, MEXICO AND THE UNITED STATES

The 2026 FIFA World Cup will be hosted by three countries for the first time in the tournament’s history: Canada, Mexico and the United States. Matches will be played across multiple host cities in North America, giving this edition the widest geographic footprint ever.

WORLD CUP 2026 TOURNAMENT FORMAT

The expanded format introduces a new competition structure:

12 groups of 4 teams
The top two teams from each group qualify automatically (24 teams)
The eight best third-placed teams also advance (8 teams)

This creates a Round of 32, followed by the knockout stages: Round of 16, Quarter-Finals, Semi-Finals and Final.

REIGNING WORLD CUP CHAMPIONS

Argentina enter the 2026 World Cup as the reigning champions, following their victory at the 2022 tournament.

WORLD CUP 2026 BETTING MARKETS

World Cup betting includes a wide range of markets beyond the outright winner, allowing different approaches depending on strategy and risk profile.

TOURNAMENT AND FUTURES MARKETS
World Cup Winner
To Reach the Final, Semi-Final or Quarter-Final
Stage of Elimination
Group Winner
To Qualify from the Group
Top Goalscorer (Golden Boot)
MATCH BETTING MARKETS
Match Result (1X2)
Both Teams to Score
Totals (Over/Under)
Correct Score
Half-Time / Full-Time
Handicaps
LIVE (IN-PLAY) BETTING

Live betting markets typically include:

Next Team to Score
Next Goalscorer
Live Match Result
Live Totals (Over/Under)

Live odds update continuously based on match events, momentum and tactical decisions.

LAST 10 WORLD CUP WINNERS
Year	Host Country	Winner	Runner-Up
2022	Qatar	Argentina	France
2018	Russia	France	Croatia
2014	Brazil	Germany	Argentina
2010	South Africa	Spain	Netherlands
2006	Germany	Italy	France
2002	South Korea/Japan	Brazil	Germany
1998	France	France	Brazil
1994	United States	Brazil	Italy
1990	Italy	West Germany	Argentina
1986	Mexico	Argentina	West Germany
WORLD CUP TOP GOALSCORER

Who will collect the Golden Boot at the 2026 World Cup? Will it be a superstar youngster like Bukayo Saka or Argentina’s Julian Alvarez? What impact will megastars Erling Haaland and Kylian Mbappé have? Or will someone from the veteran side of things like England’s Harry Kane, Brazil’s Neymar or the great Lionel Messi do the business?
